<div id="top_blog" data-beacon='{"p":{"mnid":"topBlog","plid":1432795,"mpid":1}}'>
	<div class="entry no_border" id="blog_1432795" onmouseover="TrackingData.blog_1432795={id:1432795,blog_id:3,rank:1,zone:4,vertical:-1,ab_headline:'a'};">
		<div class="top_blog">
			<div class="first_blog_headshot">
								<a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/doug-kendall"><img src="http://s.huffpost.com/contributors/doug-kendall/headshot.jpg" width="45" height="45" alt="Doug Kendall" /></a><br />
				
			</div>
			<div class="col entry_right">
				<h3><a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/doug-kendall/what-a-conservative-judic_b_1432795.html">Doug Kendall: What a Conservative Judicial Revolution Looks Like</a></h3>
			</div>
			
			<p class="author_teaser">Founder and President, Constitutional Accountability Center</p>			
			
								<p>As the Supreme Court's conservative majority stands poised at the edge of a cliff -- debating whether or not to strike down the Affordable Care Act and pick a very large fight with Congress and a sitting President -- two conservative judges on the U.S. Court of Appeals for the D.C. Circuit sought to push them over the edge last week. Their opinion -- a startling call for the abandonment of eight decades of Supreme Court case law in economic cases and a return to the pre-New Deal "Lochner Era" -- is the clearest roadmap yet as to what a conservative judicial revolution looks like.</p>
			
			
			<div class="entry_meta">
				<p>
					<a class="read_post_link" href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/doug-kendall/what-a-conservative-judic_b_1432795.html">Read Post</a>
					| <a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/doug-kendall/what-a-conservative-judic_b_1432795.html#comments">Comments <span class="comment_count" id="blog_comment_count_1432795">(39)</span></a>
	
				</p>
			</div>
		</div>

			</div>
						<div class="clear"></div>
			
            <p class="byline_timestamp"><a href="http://www.huffingtonpost.com/ester-bloom">Ester Bloom</a>, 04/17/12</p>
            <p class="author_teaser">Freelance writer</p>

				<script type="text/javascript">
					function create_url_for_featured_posts(page) {
						var url = '';
						if($('featured_posts_module_pages_ids_'+page))
							url = '/ajax/frontpage/blog/featured_posts_page.php?vertical=homepage&page='+page+'&entries_ids='+$('featured_posts_module_pages_ids_'+page).innerHTML;
						else
							return false;
	
						return url;
					}
                    function featured_posts_pagination_callback(page) {
                        var dest = $('all_sponsored_posts_page_'+page+'_wrapper');
                        var partner_ad = $('ad_deal_lower_left_page_'+page+'_wrapper');
                        if (partner_ad && $('ad_deal_lower_left_wrapper')) {
                            partner_ad.innerHTML = $('ad_deal_lower_left_wrapper').innerHTML;
                        } 
                        if (dest && $('all_sponsored_posts')) {
                            dest.innerHTML = '<div id="all_sponsored_posts_page_'+page+'"></div>';
                            $('all_sponsored_posts_page_'+page).appendChild($('all_sponsored_posts'));
                            if ($('hp_sponsored_posts_max_page')) {
                                sponsor_blogs_pagination = new CommonPaginator({'moduleName': 'sponsored_posts', 'maxPage': parseInt($('hp_sponsored_posts_max_page').innerHTML), 'is_circle': true, 'is_ajax_update': true, 'create_page_ajax_url':create_url_for_sponsored_posts, 'update_images': true});
                            }
                        }
                        
                        if(curr_page != page) {
	                        var blog_column_edit_promo = '<div id="all_sponsored_posts_page_' + page + '_wrapper">' + jQuery('#all_sponsored_posts_page_' + page + '_wrapper').html() + '</div>';
	                        jQuery('#all_sponsored_posts_page_' + page + '_wrapper').remove();
	                        if(curr_page < page)
	                            jQuery('#hp_featured_posts_page_' + page + ' div.entry').eq(blog_column_edit_promo_position).after(blog_column_edit_promo);
	                        else
	                            jQuery('#hp_featured_posts_page_' + page + ' div.entry').eq(blog_column_edit_promo_position - 1).after(blog_column_edit_promo);
	                        curr_page = page;
                        }
                    }
                    var featured_posts_pagination = new CommonPaginator({'moduleName': 'featured_posts', 'maxPage': 4, 'is_circle': true, 'is_ajax_update': true, 'create_page_ajax_url':create_url_for_featured_posts, 'callback':featured_posts_pagination_callback, 'update_images': true});
                    huff.emit('content/update', '#hp_featured_posts_page_1');
                    
                    var curr_page = 1;
                    var blog_column_edit_promo = '<div id="all_sponsored_posts_page_1_wrapper">' + jQuery('#all_sponsored_posts_page_1_wrapper').html() + '</div>';
                    jQuery('#all_sponsored_posts_page_1_wrapper').remove();
                    jQuery('#hp_featured_posts_page_1 div.entry').eq(blog_column_edit_promo_position - 1).after(blog_column_edit_promo);
                    jQuery('#hp_featured_posts_main>.preview').remove();
				</script>

	function create_url_for_recent_blog_posts(page) {
		var url = '';
		if($('recent_blog_posts_module_pages_ids_'+page))
			url = '/ajax/frontpage/blog/recent_posts_page.php?vertical=homepage&page='+page+'&entries_ids='+$('recent_blog_posts_module_pages_ids_'+page).innerHTML;
		else
			return false;

		return url;
	}

	var recent_blog_posts = new CommonPaginator({'moduleName': 'recent_blog_posts', 'maxPage': 4, 'is_circle': true, 'is_ajax_update': true, 'create_page_ajax_url':create_url_for_recent_blog_posts, 'is_ajax_eval':true});

<script type="text/javascript">
var s2title, phone_n;

handleSendResponse = function(s) {
	console.log(JSON.stringify(s));
	console.log(s.status);
	if (s.status == 4) {
		s2title.html("Your message was sent to "+phone_n+'.');
	} else if (s.status == 5) { 
		s2title.html("Send Failed");
	} else if (s.status == 3) { 
		s2title.html("Sorry, no more messages may be sent today.");
	}
}
errorHandle = function(request, errorType, errorThrown) {
	if(errorType == 'timeout') { 
		s2title.html("Send Failed");
	}
}
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .showlegal').live('click', function(){
	if(jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2disclaimer').html() != jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2legal').html()) {
		jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2disclaimer').slideUp(500, function(){
			jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2disclaimer').html(jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2legal').html()).slideDown(500);
		});
	}
	return false;
});
jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble input[value="Send"]').live('click', function(){
	s2title = jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2title');
	phone_n = jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble input[name="p1"]').val().replace(/-/g, '');
	if(phone_n == 5555555555 || isNaN(phone_n) || phone_n.length != 10) {
		jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2subtitle').fadeOut(500, function () {
			jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2subtitle').html('Please use a valid 10-digit mobile number.').css('color', '#FF0000').fadeIn(500);
		});
		return false;
	}
	jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .s2title').html('Sending...');
	var appid = '26';
	var appkey = 'ao1qvHJSh3Z7hgQQ';
	var phone = phone_n;
	var message = 'Huffington Post for iPhone';
	var link = 'http://itunes.apple.com/us/app/huffingtonpost-com/id306621789?mt=8';
	var url = 'http://s2c.aol.com/s2c/sendtocell.jsp?appid='+encodeURIComponent(appid)+'&appkey='+encodeURIComponent(appkey)+'&phone='+encodeURIComponent(phone)+'&message='+encodeURIComponent(message)+'&link='+encodeURIComponent(link);
	console.log(url);
	jQuery.ajax({
		url: url,
		dataType: "jsonp",
		crossDomain: true,
		timeout: 15 * 1000,
		error: errorHandle
	});
	return false;
});
jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble .closable').live('click', function(){
	jQuery('#af-iphone_bubble').parent().addClass('hidden');
});
</script>
